The United States Prepares to Join with Conditions

Joins the International Court of Justice

▲Reuters report from Washington on the 12th: Senate Foreign Relations Committee Chairman Borah today reported to the Senate that he approved the amendments supporting the United States' joining the World Court. It seems that the United States is preparing to join. The United States has been hesitant to join the World Court for nine years, and three presidents have advocated that the Senate conditionally approve the articles of the World Court during these nine years. The reservations agreed upon by the United States stipulate that the court may not accept requests to handle any dispute or issue related to the interests of the United States without the express consent of the United States, and that all related countries must formally recognize the reservations of the United States, before the United States can join. Borah has strongly opposed the United States joining the World Court. There are currently 54 countries that have joined the World Court, and only 9 countries have not joined: Argentina, Mexico, Honduras, Afghanistan, Ecuador, Egypt, Soviet Russia, and the United States.

Important News

Japanese Newspaper Comments

Danger in Franco-Russian Relations

▲Because of the Assassination of President Doumer ▲Fear of Causing a Second World War The Osaka Asahi Shimbun recently published a lengthy article entitled (Fear that the Rupture of Franco-Russian Diplomatic Relations will Lead to a Second World War). The article stated that after the assassination of French President Doumer, the perpetrator confessed that he greatly admired Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and German National Socialist leader Hitler. The perpetrator seemed to be a white radical. However, before Doumer, other French presidents had been assassinated, such as Carnot on June 24, 1894, who was killed by the anarchist Caserio during an official luncheon in Lyon. This caused a national uproar in France. This time, the perpetrator who assassinated Doumer was Russian. According to the announcement by the French government, the perpetrator was not a White Russian exile, but a former Communist Party member. Therefore, Prime Minister Tardieu and other key figures have been holding secret meetings for days, and the situation is extremely tense. Moreover, Russia and France are already incompatible in terms of doctrine and policy. Recently, the two countries signed a non-aggression pact to prevent conflict, but unexpectedly, this major incident suddenly occurred. The effectiveness of that treaty is bound to vanish. In addition, the Soviet Union openly advocates revising the Treaty of Versailles for Germany and also holds the same sympathy. Germany again wants to connect with Italy to develop the European political situation. On the other hand, France firmly insists on its views regarding war debt reparations. Therefore, the two countries are already in an irreconcilable situation. Recalling the assassination of the Austrian Crown Prince in Sarajevo in 1914, which caused a great disaster, now with the assassination of Doumer as the fuse, whether Europe in 1932 will re-enact a second world war is difficult to say. However, in recent days, anti-Russian sentiment has permeated France, and the hidden danger in the future is truly unimaginable. Tanaka's Inspection of Manchuria Afterwards

Advocating Friendship with Russia

▲Also Emphasizing the Non-Aggression Treaty The Osaka Asahi Shimbun reported that former Ambassador to Russia, Mr. Tanaka Tokichi, had been ordered to inspect Manchuria for a period of one and a half months. Now that his mission has ended, he returned to Beijing on the 8th to report on his mission. In the train, he expressed his views on Manchuria, stating that the Manchurian army is insufficient for defense, and Japan should also increase its troops as soon as possible. In the future, Japan should pay attention to Manchuria not only in economic terms but also in terms of national defense. Currently, many Manchurian officials are Japanese, which is indeed appropriate. However, the reform of the Manchurian institutions should urgently abolish the "four-headed politics" at this time, establish a unified organization, and center it on the military department to take on the responsibility of maintaining law and order. Moreover, Russia has a direct relationship with Manchuria and Japan. The policy towards Russia must be very cautious, and the only urgent task is to strive for friendship and cooperation with Russia. The non-aggression treaty previously proposed by Russia should be considered with care. National Humiliation Memorial Meeting

Report by President Wang

▲People's Representative Body is Being Actively Prepared ▲The Armistice Agreement Does Not Contain Political Implications ▲Efforts to Resolve the Northeast Issue Will Be Intensified The Kuomintang Central Party Headquarters' Office in Nanjing held the May 9th National Humiliation Memorial Meeting. President Wang gave an important report, which was briefly noted in the previous report. Now, the original text of Wang's report is supplemented as follows: Comrades, today is Memorial Week and also the May 9th National Humiliation Memorial Day. The Central Party Headquarters entrusted me to report to you on the work of this past week. The important work of this past week can be divided into two parts: (1) The proceedings of the discussion regarding the National People's Congress; (2) The proceedings of the Shanghai Armistice and Troop Withdrawal Agreement. Now, I will first report on the proceedings of the discussion regarding the National People's Congress. The proposal for the National People's Congress was raised by several comrades during the First Plenary Session of this year. At that time, there were three proposals: the National Crisis Conference, the National Salvation Conference, and the National People's Congress. The First Plenary Session resolved that the National Crisis Conference should be convened by the National Government, and the National People's Congress and the National Salvation Conference should be discussed by the Standing Committee. Later, when the National Crisis Conference was held, a resolution was sent to the National Government requesting the early establishment of the National People's Congress. Therefore, the Central Political Council, for this issue, went through four detailed discussions, two formal meetings and two discussion sessions. Because this major case is very important, the Central Committee was unwilling to make a hasty decision. A formal meeting was held last Monday, and another discussion session was held on Friday. A formal meeting was held again last Monday, and another discussion session was held on Friday, so that the Central Committee would have sufficient time to discuss and exchange opinions with each other. The result of the first formal meeting was to submit the National People's Congress, the amendment proposed by Comrade Yu Youren, and the proposal for popularly elected half of the members of the Legislative and Supervisory Yuan together for review. Everyone discussed during the first discussion session. There were many key points during the discussion. Now I will report to you. One of the so-called key points is the basis. According to the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction," the foundation of civil rights should be from the bottom up. Therefore, there is Article 8 of the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" (During the period of political tutelage, the government shall send trained and qualified personnel to assist the people in each county in preparing for self-government, so as to become a fully self-governing county), and then there is Article 14 of the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" (After the establishment of local self-government in each county, one representative of the people may be elected to form a representative assembly to participate in central government affairs). Because the power of the National People's Congress is very important, it must first be established after local self-government is completed. We see that the Premier's "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" has a clear order. If we now establish the National People's Congress before self-government is completed, it would completely violate the procedures stipulated in the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction." This view has a correct reason. But at the same time, there is also a point of view that the Premier taught us a method of adapting to the times, in addition to the clear provisions of the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction." Of course, when the First National Congress of the Kuomintang was held in 1924, the Premier proposed the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction." In September, when the Premier sent troops on the Northern Expedition, he initially promulgated the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" in the name of the government, with a very long preamble attached. However, in November of the same year, when the Premier went north, he advocated convening a National Assembly. The National Assembly is also a kind of public opinion mechanism, which can prove that it is not necessary to wait until the procedures stipulated in the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" are completed before a public opinion mechanism can be established. Both of the above two key points have reasons. Therefore, after much discussion at that time, the result was that a central public opinion mechanism could be established during the period of political tutelage, but its name and powers should be discussed at the next meeting. This result was decided at the second formal meeting last Monday. When the second discussion session was held last Friday, some advocated using the name "National People's Congress," some advocated using the name "National Political Participation Council," and some advocated expanding the popularly elected members of the Legislative and Supervisory Yuan. According to the opinions of most comrades, it is more appropriate to use the name "National Political Participation Council." The reason is that the establishment of a central public opinion mechanism during the period of political tutelage is, in practice, the same as the National People's Congress. However, local self-government has not been completed. If the words "National People's Congress" are used, it would be inconsistent with the facts. Because according to the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction," each county must establish a local self-government before it can elect a member to form the National People's Congress. Now that self-government has not been completed, it is of course not the fault of the government's delay, and the people cannot be blamed. But the lack of self-government is still a fact. Ignoring the facts would inevitably contradict the "Fundamentals of National Reconstruction" established by the Premier. Therefore, everyone felt that a compromise solution was to establish a central public opinion mechanism, but change the name to "National Political Participation Council," which is consistent with the meaning of the people participating in central government affairs. However, on the one hand, the National Political Participation Council is established, and many popularly elected representatives are elected. On the other hand, the popularly elected members of the Legislative and Supervisory Yuan are still not abolished, which would become a duplicate public opinion mechanism. Therefore, everyone felt that with the establishment of the National Political Participation Council, the previous proposal for half of the members of the Legislative and Supervisory Yuan to be popularly elected could be postponed. This was the view of most comrades at the discussion session last Friday. We are preparing to summarize various opinions and make a detailed decision at the formal meeting to be held at 3:00 PM today. The situation regarding the discussion of the National People's Congress is roughly like this. This matter is a very important matter for our Party at present. To achieve the goal of completing political tutelage and promoting constitutional government, and to cultivate civil rights during the period of political tutelage, depends on the decision of this meeting. The text of the Shanghai Armistice Agreement has been disclosed in the Central Daily News and other newspapers, and the Minister of Foreign Affairs has made a declaration, which is very clear. I believe everyone has seen it. Today, what I want to say is only the two most important points: (1) Whether this agreement contains political implications; (2) Whether this agreement is separate from the Northeast issue. Regarding these two points, I can explain that if this agreement contains political implications, that is, the so-called exchange of Japanese troop withdrawal for political conditions, that would certainly lead to the danger of losing sovereignty and humiliating the country. The government absolutely refuses to do so. Fortunately, this point has been avoided. The content of the agreement does not contain political implications. Regarding the second point, if we only hope to solve the Shanghai issue and shelve the Northeast issue, that would also be a loss of sovereignty and humiliation of the country. The government also absolutely refuses to do so. We believe that the Shanghai armistice conference is only a step towards solving the Northeast issue. Some people in Shanghai say that China is a whole, so why is there an armistice and troop withdrawal in Shanghai, but not in the Northeast? It must be known that China has not declared war on Japan. If war is formally declared, of course there will be an armistice and troop withdrawal together. However, this time, the government's policy is to resist on the one hand and negotiate on the other. Therefore, no matter where Japan attacks, we will resist. If Japan stops attacking, we will stop. As long as the armistice and troop withdrawal agreement does not contain political conditions, the Shanghai armistice and troop withdrawal can be carried out simultaneously with the continued resistance in the Northeast. A political meeting must raise the entire issue of China and Japan, especially the fundamental issue, that is, the Northeast issue, for resolution. It is absolutely not the case that the Shanghai issue is resolved and the Northeast issue is ignored. Now that these two key points have been made clear, it can be known that the establishment of this agreement is certainly not a satisfactory success or the final goal, but it is not a contract that loses sovereignty and humiliates the country. As for how to solve the Northeast issue, the government can only proceed with the policy of resisting on the one hand and negotiating on the other. Regarding this point, I have the same feelings as the May 9th National Humiliation. The May 9th National Humiliation has not yet been washed away, and the Northeast issue since September 18th has not yet been resolved. The government will never relax because of the establishment of this agreement, and will intensify its efforts to fight. Military diplomacy is certainly important, but in my personal opinion, domestic affairs are even more important, because diplomacy depends on the military, and the military depends on the economy, culture, and the organization and equipment of various sciences. The economy, culture, and the organization and equipment of various sciences depend on the improvement of domestic affairs. Therefore, if domestic affairs are not improved, the economy, culture, and the organization and equipment of various sciences cannot be carried out, and military diplomacy will never be possible. Since January 28th, I and Comrade Chiang Kai-shek have discussed domestic affairs issues. Although there are various things that should be reformed, due to all aspects of the current situation, we have adopted a gentle policy. Some things, although they should be done, cannot be done. Originally, I could give many examples, but now I will just summarize and say that the policy taken in the past few months has been a gentle policy, hoping that everyone will unite to overcome the national crisis. Although there are dissatisfactions with all aspects, we must always proceed gently. Whether this point is correct or not, please criticize. Is there a contradiction between the gentle policy and the improvement of domestic affairs? Of course there is. But if we take a firm policy, although it can reduce constraints, it can also cause disunity. Therefore, we want to wait until all conditions are met before enriching our strength. This is something that everyone must pay attention to, and please criticize strictly. In short, in the current situation, we dare not relax one step. I once said at the National Crisis Conference that the government has determined a minimum limit for the current difficult situation. Above the minimum limit, we can endure. Below the minimum limit, we must resist. The ultimatum proposed by Japan on February 20th, we absolutely did not accept. The signing of this armistice and troop withdrawal agreement is for this reason. Now that we have signed the Shanghai armistice and troop withdrawal agreement, it is only a step towards solving the Northeast issue. It cannot be said that we have embarked on the road to peace. In the future, we will have to sacrifice and fight. Today is Memorial Week and also the May 9th National Humiliation Memorial Day. The situation for more than a decade is still the same. Therefore, our spirit of sacrifice and struggle should be consistent and should be intensified day by day. This is roughly what I am reporting today. The New Work of Suppressing Bandits in Jiangxi Province

Gu Weijun Surrounded by Japanese Reporters on the Haiqi

It is said that political power assists the army. According to a Nanchang dispatch, the Jiangxi Provincial Bandit Suppression Office has decided on an extremely detailed plan for completely eliminating the Red bandits. The most important point is to use political power to assist the army in suppressing the bandits and to seize the people in the bandit areas. Previously, bandit suppression relied solely on the army and lacked the assistance of political power. Therefore, every time a place was captured, there was no local military force to maintain it. As a result, the tragedy of the bandits returning after the troops left, burning and killing, was repeated. Therefore, the future work of the Security Office is to use local political power to maintain the lost land that has been recaptured, to eliminate the small remnants of bandits in various counties, and to fundamentally eradicate the forces of the Red bandits lurking in the countryside. Since Xiong Shihui, chairman of the provincial government, concurrently served as the director of the office, he has strictly supervised the counties to eliminate the small remnants of the Red bandits, eliminate their so-called county Soviet organizations, and spare no effort. At the same time, he reorganized the Republic of China Baojia police teams, watch teams, and militiamen in various counties, expanded and tightened their organizations, strengthened their forces, and unified their command. In the past two months, there have been initial results. It is said that a general mobilization to eliminate bandits will begin soon. The required firearms and ammunition have also been fully purchased and a minimum price has been set, ordering each county to raise funds for purchase. In addition, various bandit suppression programs have been formulated, such as important plans for transportation construction and rural revitalization, preparing to submit them to the bandit suppression conference for approval and implementation. ▲ Receipts Down Compared to the Same Period Last Year National News Agency Nanjing, 13th: The Ministry of Finance officially announced that the total customs revenue for the first four months of this year was 61,847,918.64 Shanghai taels, which is lower than the 82,443,990.22 Shanghai taels for the same period last year, a shortfall of 20,596,071.58 Shanghai taels.

▲The Shanghai Money Trade Association will be closed for one day on June 1st. Xiao's Mother Left Shanghai Yesterday

▲Never Forget China's Hospitality ▲Extensively Promote After Returning Home The mother of the martyr Xiao De, Madam Xiao, and her second son, Edmund, boarded a ship from the Xinkuan Wharf yesterday afternoon to return to their country. Those who came to the wharf to see them off included Guo Fu representative Tang Haian, Ministry of Finance representative Zheng Lai, Municipal Government representative Yu Hongjun, Commendation Committee members Hu Yunqiu, Hu Yunzhuang, Mei Qiju, He Yongyun, Chen Boquan, Huang Tanfu, Liang Shichun, Shen Dexie, various groups' National Salvation United Association Yin Zhiling, Municipal Association Hu Feng

The Grand Farewell of Xiao's Mother by All Circles at Xinkuan Wharf

(Photo donated by Mr. Jiang Bingnan) Xiang, Road Association Cai Xiaobai, Telegraph Association Yao ShouKang, General Labour Union Chen Peide, and more than 100 representatives from over 90 organizations, as well as dozens of Moor Hall Boy Scouts. The organizations presented flower baskets, including the National Salvation United Association, Commendation Committee, General Labour Union, Telegraph Association, Road Association, National Disaster Relief Association, and more than a dozen others. Madam Xiao arrived at the wharf at 12:00 noon from the Cathay Hotel in the same car as Tang Haian, Madam Li Jinglun, and others. She shook hands with each of the representatives who came to see her off before boarding the ship. The representatives elected Yin Zhiling, Chen Boquan, and Madam Li to escort Madam Xiao to the McKinley mail ship at Bailianjing. Yin Zhiling asked Madam Xiao about her feelings after coming to Shanghai on the ship. Madam Xiao replied, "After I came to Shanghai, I received grand receptions from the Chinese government and various groups in Shanghai, and Xiao De was buried, and received a grand funeral. This not only makes me never forget China's hospitality, but also shows that Chinese society has a very deep respect for those who sacrificed for the anti-Japanese cause. I sincerely hope that more Chinese soldiers and people in the world will be willing to sacrifice their lives like Xiao De, and will receive the same grand respect and hospitality from the Chinese state and society that has been given to me. After I return to my country, I will extensively promote this grand hospitality given to me to my own people. I think that people in my country will definitely be excited when they hear about it, because since the Shandong issue occurred, officials and people in my country have all hated Japan for destroying international conventions, and have been thinking about appropriate methods to resist its atrocities. But I believe that Xiao De's death is the most practical and exciting expression of cooperation between the people of China and the United States to resist Japan." Madam Xiao is in cabin number 46 in first class, and is expected to arrive in the United States in about two weeks. The Japanese Post Office sent a ship to transport the goods.

Over 50,000 Tons of Japanese Goods

▲Osaka-Kobe Route Restored After the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, the Osaka-Kobe-Shanghai and Yokohama-Shanghai routes of the Japanese Post Office were completely suspended. The ships were transferred to Shanghai for military transport. Now, due to the withdrawal of the Japanese army and navy stationed in Shanghai, there are a large number of Japanese goods, more than 50,000 tons, left in the Osaka-Kobe area, which urgently need to be transported to Shanghai. Yesterday, the Japanese Post Office received a telegram from Tokyo, stating that in order to meet the needs of commercial transport, starting tomorrow, the Osaka-Kobe route, which had been suspended for six weeks, would be restored, with the first ship, Rokko Maru, departing. Aso Maru, Ikoma Maru, Kasagi Maru, Maya Maru, and others will also resume their routes.

Reduced Inland Waterways Ferry Services

▲Already Under Discussion Shanghai's inland waterway ferry industry experienced a surge in business after the outbreak of the war. The number of temporary ferry routes to Suzhou, Wuxi, and Changshu increased to dozens, with a total of more than 60 ships departing daily, a tenfold increase compared to before. The business was very profitable. Now, due to the withdrawal of the Japanese army and the upcoming opening of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, the temporary inland waterway ferry routes are all planning to withdraw and suspend operations. Once the train service resumes, they will return to their original state. Only one ferry each from China Merchants and Yuantong will remain on the Suzhou-Shanghai route, and the rest will cease operations.

Provincial Government Allocates Emergency Relief Funds for Farmers in Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan

▲A Total of 300,000 Yuan This time, when Japanese soldiers invaded, Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan counties all suffered devastation. The number of houses, appliances, and the lives and property of the people destroyed by Japanese soldiers' artillery and bombs is unknown. Fortunately, the local gentry and merchants established disaster relief associations one after another. They found that the farmers suffered the most. Not only were their appliances and seeds lost, but also the capital to engage in farming after the Japanese soldiers withdrew was nowhere to be found. The associations, in view of this, used the names of the Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan County Disaster Relief Associations to petition the provincial government for relief. It is said that the petition has been approved, and 100,000 yuan in cash has been allocated to provide emergency relief to farmers in Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan counties. In addition, Suzhou Province's busy canal mortgage loan vouchers (with a face value of 300,000 yuan) will be used to borrow 200,000 yuan in cash, which will be issued to the disaster relief associations in the three counties to provide relief, so that they can engage in farming.

Liu Zhi, chairman of Henan Province, took a row of guards at 3:10 pm yesterday and went to the South Station by car. The South Station Master dispatched a bus and attached it to the 38th Express Train to Hangzhou. It is reported that Liu met with Chen Mingshu in Hangzhou, and will need to stay in Hangzhou for several days before turning to Beijing to return to Henan.

French Ambassador to China, Mr. Wilden, came to Shanghai to participate in the Sino-Japanese ceasefire conference, and has been stationed for nearly two months. It is known that Ambassador Wilden took the British ship Changsha last night to leave Shanghai for Beijing for official business. He plans to stay in Beijing for one or two days, and will then go north to Ping via the Jinpu Railway.

The British Boxer Indemnity Committee will hold a meeting in Shanghai

▲Completing the Yuehan Railway, Managing Students Studying Abroad The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors is scheduled to hold its 7th regular meeting and 9th general meeting in Shanghai on the 16th and 18th. It is reported that the important proposals at this meeting are: (1) The Ministry of Railways requests a loan of £170,000 to complete the Yuehan Railway project; (2) The Ministry of Industry's Central Machinery Plant's £120,000 loan guarantee interest and repayment method; (3) Regulations for handling loan requests. In addition, the association previously received a request for assistance from students studying in the United Kingdom from the three northeastern provinces. The association believed that there were no funds available for the time being. Chairman Zhu Jiahua telegraphed the Chinese Committee of various universities in London to find a way to provide assistance nearby. According to Mr. Hang Liwu, Director-General of the British Boxer Indemnity Committee, the committee has agreed to allocate £500 in advance to lend to the students.

The Northeast Righteous Army Sends Representatives to Shanghai

▲Report on the Anti-Japanese Course ▲And Ask All Circles for Assistance The 10th Route of the Liaoning Righteous Army is formed by the old troops and militia of various parts of the Northeast. The commander is Wu Chaogang. It currently has more than 20,000 cavalry and infantry. Since the Shenyang Incident, it has repeatedly fought fiercely with the Japanese aggressors and has won considerable victories. However, due to the harsh environment and the lack of supplies and bullets, it has not been able to fight the Japanese army to the death. Taxpayer Association Writes to the Public Works Department

Correcting the New Regulations for Water Supply ▲The Real Estate Association will hold a meeting today to discuss After the British-owned water company in the Public Concession implemented the water meter system, the Real Estate Association opposed collecting and resolving water fees on its behalf. It specifically scheduled a general meeting of members at 3:00 pm today at No. 98 Beijing Road, to discuss the method. The Citizens' United Association, on the other hand, opposes water meters and demands the restoration of the package water system. The Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the Director-General of the Public Works Department yesterday to correct the new regulations of the water company. The original letter stated, "Sir, according to a letter from resident He Lihua, the water company in this concession has revised its new regulations. All users with water meters must use 10,000 gallons or more. For those who use more, it will be added incrementally, and for those who use less, it will be calculated according to 10,000 gallons. The price per thousand gallons is 62.5 cents. This kind of cutting the feet to fit the shoes is not a concern for the rich, but it will inevitably cause great difficulties in the lives of small families. For users who do not use 10,000 gallons, and want to pay the high price of 10,000 gallons, how can they calculate the losses that accumulate over the years? Using water is not as insignificant as the bus ticket price, or you can choose not to take it. Business in the business world relies entirely on fairness. The company's new regulations not only make it difficult for individuals, but also affect the market. I hereby request that you find a way to advocate so that users in the concession can reduce their burden. After the meeting, this matter has a great impact on the living expenses of users in the concession. The bureau should immediately implement the correction of the fair agency.

The Ninth Health Campaign

▲Focus on the Grand Cleaning of Zhabei The 15th of this month is the date stipulated by the central government for the national health campaign and grand cleaning. The city's Health Bureau has been planning and holding publicity and implementation of essential methods related to hygiene every year, which has been able to awaken a considerable awareness of public health among citizens. This is the city's ninth health campaign. It is heard that the Municipal Health Bureau, in view of the post-war epidemic, believes that the work of preventing epidemics and cleaning up the filth in the war zone is very important. The bureau has drafted methods and submitted them to the municipal government for review. The municipal government believes that cleaning up the filth in the war zone is the top priority, and has instructed the bureau to instruct this health campaign to focus on the grand cleaning of Zhabei and other war zones. The bureau, after receiving the order, immediately stepped up preparations and is now ready to be held on schedule. Zhabei

Restoration of Water and Electricity Projects

The Zhabei Water and Electricity Company temporarily moved to Ningbo Road during the war. It is now known that it has moved back to its original general office at Arui Lane, North Sichuan Road. All water pipes and electric wires damaged by artillery fire in the Zhabei area, except for those that were completely destroyed and had no residents, have been repaired by engineers and craftsmen since the end of the war. Now, tap water, electricity, and power can be supplied as usual. At the end of last month, the maximum power supply load reached 7,188 kilowatts, while the load in the same month last year was 11,744 kilowatts, which has recovered more than 60%. The daily delivery of tap water is 4 million gallons, which is about 45% of the original supply. Recently, with the signing of the ceasefire agreement, many residents have moved back, and the number of households requesting to connect to water and electricity every day is very large. The company's business prospects will continue to improve.

▲A Special Committee Will Be Established Representatives of the Municipal Citizens' Rent Reduction and Exemption Movement Committee, Yu Hualong, Zhang Yichen, Li Yongxiang, and others went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau at 10:00 am yesterday (the 13th) to request Director Mai Chaoshu of the bureau to issue laws and regulations on the issue of rent reduction and exemption in various areas affected by the war, so that the public can follow. As for the concession, no matter the court or the Public Works Department, there will be concrete measures based on government orders, so there will be no problems. According to Director Mai, the bureau had already submitted this case to the municipal government and reviewed the regulations for organizing the committee. It has been instructed to plan for the bureau, but the government is afraid that it will not be able to do so thoroughly, so it is requested that relevant groups also add representatives to jointly organize the establishment of the committee.

Change the Method of Increasing Postage

▲Decision to Start from the 20th of This Month The Japanese newspaper, Nichinichi Shimbun, reports: Since the postage increase on the first of this month, the new regulations have been used. People from all walks of life believe that at a time when the social economy is increasingly bankrupt, the government has not provided relief, but has increased the burden on the people, and has been criticized by the masses. In order to comply with public sentiment, the Executive Yuan decided to order the Ministry of Transportation to reduce the increase in the new regulations and handle them in a flexible manner, so that the people would increase slightly without harm, and the postal service could expand by this. Yesterday, the person in charge of the Postal Administration told a Nichinichi Shimbun reporter that the Postal Administration had received an order from the Ministry of Transportation the day before yesterday regarding this change of method, and would begin to implement it from the 20th of this month. After implementation, it will no longer be changed. The various methods are recorded as follows: Add 1 cent in this city (2 cents per letter), change to add 1 cent in other cities (5 cents per letter), add 1 cent for postcards in this city (that is, 2 cents), change to add half a cent for postcards in other cities (2.5 cents), express mail (express mail does not add postage, it is handled as ordinary mail, that is, 17 cents), single registration changes to add 2 cents, including postage, each letter is a total of 13 cents, double registration (registration fee plus 4 cents, including postage a total of 21 cents), fees for books, etc. are not added, everywhere

Exemption from the Spring and Summer Patrol Donations

▲More than 100 Stores Jointly Signed a Letter of Request ▲The Citizens' Branch Announces that it will Strive for It One Hundred and Twenty-two stores on North Sichuan Road requested exemption from the spring and summer patrol donations, and jointly signed and sealed a letter to the Citizens' 17th District Branch for assistance. The association immediately forwarded the letter to the Taxpayers' Association for unanimous support, and also notified members yesterday. The letter is recorded below: ▲Stores jointly request This time, the citizens of our district have suffered from the destruction of the Japanese army. In February and March, nine out of ten houses were empty, and there was no sound of chickens or dogs. The streets were like wash. Although there have been successive returns in the past half month, the terror has not been eliminated, and dangerous situations are arising. There is no time to seek a livelihood, let alone to restore business. The cause of today's unprecedented catastrophe is that the Public Works Department easily handed over police power to the Japanese, resulting in this. From this observation, the obligation of taxpayers has been fulfilled, but the rights of taxpayers are like this. The exemption of patrol donations for two seasons is not an extravagance. The following signed store owners are determined to urge the Chinese directors of the Taxpayers' Association to actively negotiate and strive for victory. It is heard that the Public Works Department intends to divide the roads north of Suzhou Creek into grades, such as north of Peng Road, which is considered to have more severe disaster, and south of Peng Road, which is considered to have less severe disaster. But is the human hell of Sanyuan Temple on East Wuchang Road, and the repeated fires of Qingyun Lane, a fact that the disaster is less severe? Any resolutions made by the Public Works Department, if they have not obtained the consent of merchants and others, will be resolutely resisted. In particular, it is co-signed to the left, and it is hoped that your branch will advocate for justice. Since the Shanghai Incident occurred, the losses suffered by Chinese merchants and citizens cannot be counted. The most serious losses were suffered by the citizens of our 17th district. Tracing the source, the Japanese soldiers occupied the public concession north of Suzhou Creek as a military base. The Public Works Department could neither take effective sanctions nor express the expulsion of Japanese soldiers from the country, resulting in an unprecedented tragedy. The Public Works Department abandoned its duties, and the blame is undeniable. In view of this, the branch of this district has to run around and shout, urging the Chinese directors of the Taxpayers' Association to uphold justice and negotiate seriously with the Public Works Department, demanding compensation for losses, and at the same time requesting exemption from the spring and summer patrol donations to show preferential treatment. Who knows that on May 11th, the report stated that the Public Works Department's proposed methods for reducing and exempting municipal donations set the highest limit for special circumstances at three months, and the rest were divided into two months, one and a half months, and so on. Tracing back to the suffering and magnitude of the damage suffered by the region under the ravages of the Japanese army, after the ceasefire conference was concluded, it still felt painful to think about the past and it was not easy to recover. However, in the end, who should bear the responsibility? The truth is also very clear. Now, the Public Works Department insists on the number of months of exemption from the trivial patrol donations, which is not worth the candle. How can it be said to be appropriate in terms of law and reason? Therefore, our association, on behalf of the members of this region, continues to insist on the previous claim and strive to fight. In addition to having sent a letter to the Chinese Taxpayer Association to work together, this is hereby notified.

Medical and Nursing News After the Cessation of Hostilities

Since the outbreak of war in the city, it has been three months, and the intense warfare has also lasted for several months. Our soldiers and refugees have suffered extremely heavy casualties. The hospitals in various places are all overcrowded, and it is even more difficult to allocate the number of doctors and nurses. The Hong Kong Branch of the Chinese Medical Association, in view of the needs of the situation, specially invited well-known medical and nursing groups in Hong Kong to organize the Hong Kong Chinese Doctors' Relief Committee. Doctors Feng Qingyou, nurses Gan Shufang, and 28 others came to Shanghai to serve. All the staff stayed at the Chinese Medical Association's new association at No. 7 Awenyi Road, Chi Pond Road. The entire upper floor of the association building was used as a dormitory for the doctors and nurses, and the rooms on the lower floor were used as reception rooms and dining rooms. All kinds of utensils for food, bedding, entertainment, etc. were temporarily set up, and everything was available. All expenses were covered by the Medical Association. The group stayed in Shanghai for more than two months and served in the First Hospital hosted by the Citizens' Maintenance Association, with remarkable achievements. Now that the war has ceased and the medical work has all ended, the patients who have not recovered have been transferred to formal hospitals in various places for treatment. The doctors and nurses will buy oars and return to Hong Kong this morning. It is heard that Dr. Niu Huisheng, president of the Medical Association, held a grand banquet last night at 7:00 p.m. to bid farewell and answer the high friendship.

Local News Two

Inside Story of Opium Public Sales

▲ Remarks from an Official of the Anti-Opium Association

The Chinese National Anti-Opium Association, in light of the widespread implementation of opium public sales in various provinces in both the North and South, and the rumors of central government involvement, has united with various public organizations to launch protests. The situation has been reported in various newspapers. A reporter from the National Communications Agency, recognizing the implications of opium public sales on national honor and public health, specifically interviewed a key official of the association to discuss the matter. The following is a summary of the conversation:

(Question) The talk of opium public sales has been circulating for several years. Could you share the details of its development?

(Answer) Opium public sales have always been the most effective method for imperialists to invade and weaken smaller nations, killing to enrich themselves. Even a child knows the poison of this scheme. No country in the world would implement it domestically. In recent years, our country has been plagued by internal strife, and some unscrupulous warlords have repeatedly implemented it for profit. Although the central government has been unable to stop it, its harm has been limited to a small area and for a relatively short period. The central government has consistently expressed its commitment to the anti-opium legacy of Sun Yat-sen and the traditional policy of prohibition. The central government previously implemented public sales but, due to public opposition and the correction by honest officials, it was soon canceled. Unexpectedly, since Liu Ruiheng became the head of the Smoking Prohibition Committee last year, he has been seeking to curry favor with certain authorities and to advance his personal interests. He deliberately implemented opium public sales, even enlisting Li Jihong, who previously handled the opium special tax in Hunan and Hubei, and using Wu Lien-te to advocate for opium public sales in order to confuse public opinion. The subsequent erratic behavior of the Prohibition Investigation Office revealed the truth, which the public should still remember. Although it was canceled due to public opposition, Liu, Wu, and their ilk were extremely unwilling to let go of such a lucrative opportunity. They have been strenuously plotting the revival of public sales, leading to the strange phenomenon of public sales in various provinces. The harms of opium public sales are so obvious. It is outrageous that so-called intellectuals and medical doctors like Liu and Wu would openly promote it, sacrificing the nation and its people for their personal gain and advancement. This is truly a rare and bizarre spectacle in these degenerate times. Our association is committed to advocating for the public, and we are deeply saddened by this situation. We feel it is our responsibility to firmly oppose it, and there is absolutely no political or factional agenda involved.

(Question) What is your association's stance on opposing public sales, and what steps are you taking?

(Answer) Our association's stance on opposing public sales has been consistent from the start and will not waver due to environmental influences. We are prepared to face any oppression or sacrifice, as we have been entrusted by society with the important mission of anti-opium advocacy. The public's sympathy and trust in our association are growing daily, and our determination to fight is strengthening with time. For example, last year, due to our opposition to public sales, our General Secretary Huang Jia-hui and his wife were falsely accused of opium trafficking. Huang narrowly escaped assassination while investigating in Taiwan and returning to the mainland. At the same time, our association faced various serious and illegal forms of oppression. However, our members have not been discouraged but have become even more courageous. The public clearly understands the nature of those who harm us, and the number of those who share our views is constantly increasing. If our members unfortunately fall victim to the enemy's plots, we know that those who rise up in our place will be ten or a hundred times more numerous. We are fighting for justice, so what is there to fear? As for our steps to oppose public sales, they are very simple. Our backing is public opinion, and our weapon is public opinion. Our steps are nothing more than to arouse public sympathy, unify public opinion, use public opinion to supervise the government, and use public opinion to drive out those shameless opium peddlers and corrupt officials.

(Question) Could you provide some recent updates on the progress of public sales?

(Answer) The recent public sales in various provinces would not have been possible without the instigation or approval of the central government's anti-opium authorities. Currently, the central anti-opium authorities are planning public sales in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Wu Lien-te, the originator of public sales, has been traveling frequently between Beijing and Shanghai, secretly lobbying for this matter. According to reports, the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Director Shu recently came to Shanghai and agreed on a fixed price of one million yuan per month with a representative of a certain silver company named Lu. It is expected to be implemented soon. We sincerely hope that all parties will rise up to protest and closely monitor this, so that the monsters under the bright sun dare not show their faces. It is a fortunate thing for opium prohibition.

(Question) It is said that there are international machinations behind the central government's implementation of opium public sales. Does your association have any information on this?

(Answer) We have not only heard about it but also know it in great detail. However, this matter is very complex and concerns national honor. We will not disclose it until it is absolutely necessary. We will discuss it in detail in the future.

Hua 界 Nine Acres

Opium Organization Established

▲ Mayor Wu Secretly Orders Thorough Investigation

Mayor Wu Tiecheng has recently received several confidential reports stating that a large-scale organization for selling opium has been established near the Nine Acres area of the Chinese district. It is now fully operational and conducting business openly, which is a violation of the ban. With rumors of opium public sales circulating everywhere, and Shanghai being a focal point for international attention, a thorough investigation is required to eradicate the source of the problem. It is reported that Mayor Wu has secretly instructed the Municipal Public Security Bureau to conduct a strict investigation.

County Government

Provisional County Government Meeting Held Yesterday

▲ Discussing Preparatory Procedures for Relocation

The construction project for Shanghai County's relocation to Beiqiao is scheduled to start with a public tender on the 16th of this month (tomorrow) and will be opened on June 1st. To prepare for the bidding process, the county government convened a provisional county government meeting yesterday, chaired by County Magistrate Yan. The meeting discussed the preparatory procedures at length and considered whether to tender for the new government buildings, roads, and bridges simultaneously. It was decided that the buildings and roads would be tendered first, while the bridges would be postponed. The meeting then adjourned.

Citizens' Association for Promoting National Products

Introducing Overseas Chinese to Visit National Product Factories

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for Promoting National Products is introducing Zheng Bulun, the representative of the Chinese National Products Company from Cirebon, Java, to visit national product factories. Letters have been sent to various factories stating:

"This association received a letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce on the 13th of this month, which stated, 'Greetings. On the 12th of this month, we received instruction No. 2161 from the Bureau of Social Affairs, which stated, "We received instruction No. 11265 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which stated, 'According to a report from Song Faxiang, the Consul-General in Java, the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Cirebon, Java, reported that overseas Chinese residents desire to purchase national products but suffer from a shortage of supply. Recognizing this, the Chamber has responded to the demands of the times and, together with a number of substantial merchants, plans to establish a large-scale national products company to purchase national products in bulk and sell them overseas. However, those who have been engaged in the national products business in Southeast Asia are largely unaware of the domestic market situation, resulting in goods that are of poor quality or unsuitable for the Southeast Asian market, leading to many failures. The Chamber has learned from past experiences and has selected Zheng Bulun to travel to China in April and May to investigate the production and sales of national products in Guangzhou, Xiamen, Fuzhou, Shanghai, Hangzhou, Nanjing, Hankou, Kaifeng, Beiping, Tianjin, Jinan, and other places, to serve as a standard for future purchases. We therefore request that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce be asked to instruct the relevant departments and chambers of commerce in the aforementioned provinces and cities to introduce Zheng to visit various national product factories upon his arrival and provide him with all kinds of conveniences." Please review and implement as appropriate. Upon investigation, the Chamber of Commerce in Cirebon's plan to organize a national products company to promote national products is indeed a matter of urgency. National product manufacturers in various regions should take advantage of Zheng Bulun's return to China to investigate, properly guide his visit, and widely provide information on national product manufacturing and promotional materials to encourage promotion. According to the report, in addition to instructing and separately ordering, we hereby order the bureau to send personnel and instruct the various national product companies and factories to comply. Upon Zheng Bulun's arrival, properly receive him and guide his visit, this order, etc., has been received. This association hereby informs you to comply, send personnel to properly receive him at the appropriate time, guide the visit, and notify all national product companies and factories to comply, etc.,' Upon receiving this instruction, this association will send personnel to guide the visit at the appropriate time and send separate letters. We hereby inform you to comply, etc. It is the sole duty of this association to promote foreign trade. Having received the aforementioned letter, this association, in addition to appointing Chen Binghui, Xu, Jianruo, and Fang Jiange to receive and guide the visit at the appropriate time, hereby informs you to take note, etc."

Renowned British Merchant

Lee's Cause of Death Unknown

▲ Police Suspect Disappearance and Begin Search ▲ Body Suddenly Found on North Suzhou Road

The Zi Lin Bao (North-China Daily News) reports that yesterday morning (12th), a watchman spotted a renowned British merchant, Lee, dead on the side of North Suzhou Road. His limbs were broken, and it appeared that he had fallen from the balcony of the Astor House Hotel. His body was half on the sidewalk and half in the street. The Hongkou police were immediately notified and dispatched officers to the scene. Dr. Wolffe also arrived in response to the call. Upon examination, Lee was already dead, with a fractured neck being the apparent cause of death. The coroner of the British Consulate examined the body yesterday afternoon and adjourned the inquest. The police are currently investigating the cause of death. According to official sources, the deceased resided on Yuanmingyuan Road but had been missing since the 3rd of this month. Although he had been spotted several times, his whereabouts were unknown. The police had recently listed him as a missing person and began searching for him this Wednesday. Therefore, there are many suspicions in this case. According to the watchman, the deceased was not seen entering the building. It is unknown whether his death was due to a fall, being pushed, or suicide.

Ren Zhennan

Judgment in Fraud Case Appealed

▲ Original Sentence Doubled ▲ Eight Months Imprisonment

Lawyer Ren Zhennan previously defended Yong businessman Zhuang Chunfu in the public court against Huang Lianxiang's charge of bigamy. Afterwards, Zhuang Chunfu claimed that he had paid Ren over 5,000 yuan in settlement fees and handling fees, but Ren had not settled the case, causing him to suffer imprisonment. He was eventually released after another settlement. Therefore, Zhuang accused Ren of fraud and requested the Lawyers' Association to request the local court to investigate and publicly prosecute Ren. The court sentenced Ren Zhennan to four months imprisonment and ordered him to compensate Zhuang Chunfu for the loss of over 5,000 yuan. Ren was dissatisfied and appealed. After several court hearings and closing arguments, Shen Youqi, the judge, delivered the judgment yesterday, overturning the original judgment. Ren Zhennan was sentenced to eight months imprisonment for fraud, while the private prosecution portion remained the same. Ren Zhennan immediately declared his dissatisfaction with the appeal and intended to appeal again. The judge ordered him to be detained and allowed him to submit the reasons for his appeal to the higher court for review.

Sixteen Kidnappers Sentenced

▲ Qi Xian Sentenced to Death

Jin Yangwu and Xu Zhengting, the chief detective and detective of the Jing'an Temple Police Station, respectively, previously arrested sixteen male and female suspects, including kidnappers Shan Yaonan, Qi Xian, and Gu Chenshi. Four handguns and forty-six bullets were confiscated. It was found that these suspects had kidnapped Cai Guanhou, the son of Cai Shaotang, in Tianshenggang, Jingjiang, on July 2nd of last year, and had committed multiple armed robbery cases in the Public Concession. They were handed over to the First Special District Court. The police were represented by lawyer Wang Yaotang, and after more than ten court hearings, the facts were clarified, and the suspects were awaiting sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Qian Hongye announced the judgment in the Criminal Division One. Defendant Shan Yaonan was sentenced to life imprisonment, Qi Xian was sentenced to death, Zhu Qijun was sentenced to twelve years imprisonment, Li Chengzhong, Xu Xiaomei, and Li Jishi were each sentenced to six years imprisonment, Zhao Zhenghua was sentenced to thirteen years imprisonment, Ren Jinbiao was sentenced to twelve years imprisonment, Wang Hailan and Gao Xinfu were each sentenced to twelve years imprisonment, and Yang Benzhang and Zhang Yushan were each sentenced to fourteen years imprisonment. Shen Fenghao and Wang Guifang were found not guilty. Wang was temporarily detained pending extradition by Haimen County. Shen was remanded in custody pending appeal. The guns and bullets were confiscated.

Impersonating Officers to Search for Opium

▲ Extorting 140 Yuan ▲ A Special Russian Constable Involved

Lu Jinsheng, a native of Songjiang, has been working as a fruit vendor. Recently, his relatives Wu Renfu and Wu Sancheng came to Shanghai from Songjiang to seek refuge. They resided in Room 420 of the Wugong Hotel on Fuzhou Road. At 8 PM on the 11th of this month, Chen Changsheng (a local), Xu Zigen (from Wuxi), and a Russian named Leiweisiji (who works as an inspector at the telephone company and also serves as a special constable No. 60 in the Public Concession police force) suddenly broke into the room. Chen claimed that they were sent by the General Police Station to search for opium and began to search. They found a small amount of opium in a drawer and used this as an excuse to threaten them, saying that they had to be taken to the police station, otherwise, they would have to pay 300 yuan. Lu did not have such a large sum of money at the time and began to negotiate. They eventually settled on 140 yuan. Lu took out 40 yuan, and Wu Sancheng borrowed 50 yuan, totaling 90 yuan, and gave it to Chen Changsheng. The remaining 50 yuan was to be delivered to the Changle Teahouse on Fuzhou Road between 6 PM and 7 PM the following day, the 12th. Chen and the others then left with the money. Afterwards, Lu Jinsheng reported the matter to the Old Gate Police Station. The police chief ordered detectives Chen Yonggui and Ye Yusi, along with Western Detective Wilcox, to secretly go to the Changle Teahouse the day before yesterday and pretend to be tea drinkers. At 6:10 PM, Chen Changsheng, Xu Zigen, Di Chunxing, and Lu Wenzao went to Changle together. While Chen was talking to Lu, Lu handed Chen 10 yuan and was arrested by the Chinese and Western detectives. Xu, Di, and Lu were also taken into custody. 10 yuan were found on Chen and 28 yuan were found on Xu. Chen confessed that the Russian Leiweisiji was an accomplice. The Western Detective invited Lei to the police station, and Lei also admitted to the matter. Subsequently, detectives from the French Concession Police Station accompanied them to Lei's residence at 263 Avenue Albert in the French Concession, where 50 yuan were found. All were taken into custody and transferred to Criminal Division One of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. The police lawyer Qian Xunjiu presented the above situation and submitted the stolen money as evidence. The victim Lu Jinsheng also submitted a report verifying everything and pointed out that Chen, Xu, and the Russian were all in the hotel at the time, but he did not see Di and Lu. He also stated that he gave the 90 yuan to Chen. Yesterday, except for the Russian, the four went to Changle together, etc.

Chen and Xu confessed that they went to the Wugong Hotel with the Russian constable because they were informed that someone was running a large opium den with 17 opium pipes in Room 420. Lu Jinsheng voluntarily gave 90 yuan, of which 50 yuan was given to the Russian constable, and the informant took 30 yuan, with the remaining 10 yuan used for dinner. Lu also promised to give Chen a reward of 10 yuan, so he went to Changle yesterday to collect it, etc. Di Chunxing and Lu Wenzao denied the allegations, saying that they were arrested while drinking tea at Changle yesterday.

The Russian Leiweisiji confessed that he was a special constable in the police force. The previous evening, while he was passing through the Four Horses Road, Chen reported to him that someone was running a large opium den with 17 opium pipes in Room 420 of the Wugong Hotel. He went there with Chen and Xu. Upon arriving at the room, only one opium pipe and a small amount of opium were found. He did not want to make an arrest, so he left. Shortly after, Chen came after him and said that the plaintiff had given him 90 yuan and gave 50 yuan to him. He accepted it because the money had already been collected. He did not know anything about the Changle incident yesterday.

The defendants' lawyers, Fan Gang and Tan Xinzhen, requested that the defendants be released on bail pending further questioning. Judge Qian Hongye ordered Chen Changsheng, Xu Zigen, and the Russian Leiweisiji to be detained. Di Chunxing and Lu Wenzao were each released on 500 yuan bail pending further questioning on a later date.

Sending Personnel to South Asia for Investigation

Guo Yongkang, an employee of the Chinese Chemical Industry Society, departed on the Dutch mail steamer "Zhimin Canada" at 11 AM yesterday to investigate the industrial situation in South Asia and survey the promotion of industrial arts. Trial Opens in Case of Electrician Killed with Axe

▲ Widow Witnessed Defendant Committing Murder

Wu Jinsheng, a Changzhou electrician living at 25 Zhizhongli, Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, was injured and killed at home at 8 AM on the 11th of last month by four assailants with axes. The police have arrested one suspect, Zhong Afu, also known as Xiao Guangdong, and transferred him to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention. The trial continued yesterday morning in Criminal Division One, presided over by Judge Wang Gangxu. The police lawyer first reported the police investigation. When questioned, the defendant said that on the morning of that day, Ada and Zhang Jinsheng told him that they wanted to beat Wu Jinsheng. He replied that he knew Wu and could not go. They then went to commit the crime. Afterwards, he heard shouts and went to watch. He was not there at the time. His wife, Wu Wangshi, testified that a total of seven people came that day. Two people guarded downstairs, and five people went upstairs. The defendant and one person held an axe, two people held iron rods, and one person held a handgun, guarding the doorway and threatening her, prohibiting her from making any noise. The defendants then attacked and injured her husband. She witnessed it with her own eyes. One of the assailants was Jiang Da, and one was Jinsheng. She did not know the names of the others. The court found that further investigation was needed and adjourned the hearing to May 16. The defendant was detained.

Dog Bites Scrotum

▲ Health Bureau Employee Plays Carelessly

Yang Fusheng, a craftsman at the Dananmen Telephone Bureau, was returning home for lunch yesterday afternoon. As he was walking to the Huining Guild Hall at Xieqiao, he saw Li Huairen, an employee of the Health Bureau, catching dogs. He had caught a dog and was holding it by its hind legs, spinning it around as a joke. The dog became enraged and Li lost his grip. A police officer on duty took Li to the Second District Police Station. Yang was sent to the Southeast Hospital for treatment and was later sent to the Local Court for investigation.

Employees of the International Radio Station in this port, feeling that they were usually unorganized, and that in the face of national crisis, they could not resist foreign regrets without united efforts, deeply felt the urgency of unity. Underwear Weaving Factory Undertakes Bleaching and Dyeing of Cloth

The China Underwear Weaving Factory, established in 1920, has been weaving refreshing underwear fabric and fine cloth for eleven years. It has also created new styles of underwear, cool and comfortable undershirts, exquisitely designed and fashionable, which are popular both domestically and abroad. However, the factory previously outsourced the bleaching and dyeing of its cloth, which was not always satisfactory. Therefore, it was decided to add the latest bleaching and dyeing machinery after increasing shares last year. German-trained bleaching and dyeing technicians were hired, and after the equipment was manufactured and installed, it has now commenced operations with excellent results. The factory is willing to dedicate a portion of its surplus capacity to serving the community by accepting orders for bleaching and dyeing various types of cloth. It promises timely completion and affordable pricing.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Shandong coastal area will be cloudy with winds varying from southwest to northwest. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River will be cloudy with occasional rainfall or heavy fog in some areas, with winds varying from southeast to west. Due to a low-pressure system moving northeast-eastward from Jiangxi, the coastal area south of Ma'anshan Island will be cloudy with localized heavy fog and variable winds. Furthermore, the temperature in this city for the 24 hours preceding 3:00 PM yesterday reached a high of 70.5 and a low of 54.5. On the same day last year, the high was 72.5 and the low was 50.4.

Municipal Bureau of Education Prepares to

Restore Schools in War Zones

Following the January 28th Incident, schools and cultural institutions in areas such as Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and Zhenru were severely damaged. Now that the war zones are about to be gradually taken over, the Municipal Bureau of Education is actively preparing to restore the schools in these areas. The following is a brief account of the various situations: ▲Preparing to Take Over Schools in War Zones Due to traffic obstructions or occupation by Japanese troops, many schools have been unable to be managed. Now that the war zones will be gradually taken over, the Bureau of Education has sent personnel to the Takeover Committee to negotiate the takeover procedures. At the same time, all schools and cultural institutions were notified to register with the Bureau on the 14th and 15th of May. Once the takeover date is set, the Bureau will inform them by telegram to proceed with the takeover. ▲Investigating Losses Schools at all levels in the war zone have either been completely burned down or destroyed by bombing. Of the few schools that survived, they have either been used as stables by the military or looted by unscrupulous civilians. The Municipal Bureau of Education had previously investigated the losses of each school, compiled statistical tables, and sent personnel to inspect the situation. Now that the takeover has taken place, the Bureau will conduct an on-site investigation of the disaster situation of each school. ▲Planning to Restore Municipal Schools in War Zones Apart from Wusong Middle School, which had already temporarily opened in He'an Elementary School, the remaining elementary schools, some of which have been reduced to ashes and some of which have been severely damaged, cannot be opened until the damaged ones have been temporarily closed and renovated. Moreover, after the catastrophe, the local situation will inevitably be different from before. The Bureau should promptly investigate the situation of the residents and formulate a restoration plan. If school-age children have already returned to areas where schools are needed, temporary schools should be established to provide relief. Schools in the Chinese Concession

▲Notification from the Municipal Bureau of Education The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notification yesterday stating that the Shanghai Public Works Department of the Public Concession had previously proposed allocating funds to subsidize the expenses of Chinese private primary and secondary schools in the concession and had drafted subsidy regulations, seeking the Bureau's consent. Chinese to Hold Open Doubles Tournament in Early June

| Decision by the Committee of the China Tennis Club | The Committee of the China Tennis Club held its first meeting at Deng Tuomo's residence yesterday. Attendees included Hu Yunlai, Hu Xiansheng, Ling Xitao, Li Baojun, Wei Boxiang (representing Li Baojun), Zhou Jiaqi (secretary). They discussed matters related to hosting competitions and the club's constitution, among other things. The meeting adjourned after two hours. The following is an excerpt of the resolutions: (1) Hu Yunlai was elected as the chairman of the committee. (2) The club's constitution was discussed and approved. (3) It was decided to hold the Chinese Open Doubles Tournament in early June, with Hu Yunlai donating prizes to increase the interest in the competition. (4) Li Baojun was appointed as the club's manager and representative to the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association.

▲Constitution of the Shanghai China Tennis Club

(1) This club is organized by the Chinese National Sports Federation and is named the Shanghai China Tennis Club. (2) The tennis season runs from May to the end of September. (3) Membership is divided into four categories: Regular, Associate (Student), Female, and Special (Foreigner). (4) The entrance fee is 15 yuan for regular members, 12 yuan for associate members, 10 yuan for female members, and 20 yuan for special members. (5) The club provides labor, nets, and ball boys. Only members are allowed to play on the court. (6) Playing hours are from 4:00 PM daily. On Saturdays and Sundays, practice is allowed from 1:00 PM and 9:00 AM, respectively. (7) The club has a committee to manage its affairs. A secretary is appointed by the staff of the Sports Federation. (8) Members may bring friends to play tennis, but only when the court is available. Each time, they must sign the register and pay a small fee of four cents. If non-members play more than twice, the club may ask them to pay the membership fee to limit their access and avoid infringing on the rights of members. (9) To become a member, one must register and pay at the Chinese National Sports Federation on Labor Father Road, providing their address and telephone number for contact purposes. (10) Upon joining, the club will issue a membership badge, which must be worn when playing on the court for identification purposes. (11) In case of rain, wet ground, or official competitions, the club may temporarily suspend playing. (12) During official competitions, members should abide by the rules and refrain from practicing to facilitate club affairs. (13) If there are many members playing, they should take turns on the court and prioritize doubles play, with a time limit of one hour, to ensure equal opportunities and benefits for all members. (14) Shoes with heels or hard leather soles are not allowed on the court to avoid damaging the surface. (15) Players should dress neatly. Please refrain from wearing vests or long gowns to maintain a proper appearance. (16) Members should absolutely comply with the advice of the committee and club staff. This constitution may be amended at any time if it is not perfect. New and Old Billiards Championship

Lin's shooting technique was steady, and he had good fortune, ultimately winning by 500 to 472, earning the title of Billiards King, a double victory of fame and fortune. Commercial News

The silver and money industry is in the process of final closing.

Business Conditions

The silver and money industry's final closing at the end of last year has not yet been held, and has been postponed to the end of this month for summarization, as announced by the Chamber of Commerce. As citizens are uniformly following this, the silver and money industry has been rushing to complete the closing procedures recently, and is extremely busy, with no time to attend to other new development plans. Even the most critical silkworm cocoon trade is being neglected. They are only actively pursuing the redemption of previously mortgaged silk cocoons. If borrowers cannot repay, they either transfer the debt to Shanghai, pursue the guarantor for compensation, or sell the collateral. However, there are no overly harsh coercive actions. From the silver and money industry's perspective, strict collection should be enforced to facilitate adjustment. However, observing the market situation, there are indeed difficulties, and they dare not make excessive demands to avoid criticism. Therefore, they are following the trend, collecting what they can and leaving the rest alone.

Cotton Yarn and Cotton Market Slightly Soft

The cotton yarn market showed a slight softening, with fewer spot sales. Over the past three to four days, various groups have purchased a total of approximately 40,000 bales. It is expected that there may be a temporary halt, which is not surprising. Therefore, selling prices remain firm, and factories are maintaining a strong stance, as they have sold off a significant amount of their inventory. However, the Guangdong buyers have stopped purchasing, indicating a saturated demand. Jiangxi buyers, however, remain active. Market sentiment is mixed, with differing views on whether prices will rise or fall. However, based on actual observations, there is unlikely to be a strong upward trend, as the surrounding environment is not entirely optimistic, the domestic economic situation remains difficult to circulate, and Japanese factories are aggressively increasing production with cheap raw materials. Therefore, Chinese factories should take advantage of this opportunity to sell as much as possible.

Silk and Tea: Poor Condition of Spring Silkworms in Jiaxing

▲ Early Batch Already in Great Sleep, Cold Weather Prevents Emergence

Farmers in the four rural districts of Jiaxing have greatly reduced silkworm rearing this year due to economic panic. After collecting the silkworm eggs, the weather suddenly turned cold and hot, with continuous rain, which severely affected the silkworms. During the third molt, the silkworms turned yellow and suffered from rotten abdomens due to a day and night of sultry heat followed by thunderstorms, and many were discarded. The early batch is already in the great sleep (4th molt), but the extremely cold weather is preventing them from emerging. The late silkworms are only in the third molt, with vigorous leaf consumption, but development is delayed, and the situation is poor.

Selected Raw Silk Maintains Strong Prices

Yesterday, the silk market in this port remained lifeless. European and American markets saw sluggish sales of White Filature and other brands, and prices continued to weaken. Few telegraphic orders were forwarded to Shanghai, and market sentiment was depressed. However, the Shanghai stock of selected raw silk remained thin. Chinese silk merchants held firm and prices held. Yesterday, Xinfu and others imported 30 bales of "Lin Ma" brand top-grade No. 2 Zhili white raw silk at a price of 765 taels. Zhonghe imported 10 bales of "Gong He" brand top-grade No. 1 Zhili white raw silk at a price of 680 taels.

Tea Market Sales Brisk, Prices Fall

Yesterday, the tea market in this port saw brisk sales of green tea from both domestic and foreign firms. English firms such as Jinlong, Xiehe, Yihuo, and Tongfu were all stocking up, and the outflow seemed active. The entire market reached sales of over 400 chests. Tea from Suian fetched a price of around 140 taels, while domestic teas ranged from 100 to 115 taels, a decrease of 10-20 taels compared to the previous day. The current decline in tea prices is due to the soaring overseas silver prices, high exchange rates, and the lack of mail ships departing recently, leading merchants to be unwilling to hoard. With lower tea prices, sales have resumed, and the tea market trend is gradually normalizing.

"Peacock" was priced at 7 taels and 5 fen, "People with Guns Blue Chicken" at 7 taels and 1.5 qian, and "Double Tiger" at 6 taels and 8.5 qian. Ningbo, Taizhou, Guangdong and other groups are all waiting and seeing.
