Free Discussion

On Irish Freeman (Middle)

— Kai Xu

The father of the new Irish President, Mr. Eamon de Valera, was Spanish, and his mother was Irish. Therefore, what he inherited innately was a romantic and strong personality, as mentioned above. Therefore, Mr. de Valera's life story is full of twists and turns, and many strange anecdotes. But the most commendable thing among them is his prison escape in 1919, because it is an expression of the Irish national spirit of strength and romance. Mr. de Valera was arrested several times and almost died. But he was never killed, as if there was providence in it. In the spring of 1916, a revolution against the British took place in Dublin, the capital of Ireland. Mr. de Valera and his party were all arrested and imprisoned. Later, those who were imprisoned with Mr. de Valera were successively shot and martyred. However, Mr. de Valera was not immediately subjected to the death penalty because he was born in New York and had American nationality. The following year, he was released under amnesty. After his release, Mr. de Valera immediately summoned his subordinates, reorganized the (Sinn Fein) party, and expanded its revolutionary movement. Therefore, in May 1918, he was arrested again for inciting riots and imprisoned in Lincoln Prison in Ireland. Mr. de Valera's imprisonment this time was feared to be for life. Because Irish public sentiment was boiling at that time, and revolutionary ideas were rampant throughout the country. The British government treated Mr. de Valera like it treats Gandhi in India today. It was impossible to let him go, and it was impossible to kill him. So there was only the way of imprisonment. After Mr. de Valera was imprisoned, his party members wanted to get him out. So there was an organization of a committee. The committee selected dozens of daredevils who were able to go through fire and water. They were all capable of fighting to the death. They planned to rob the prison and release him. However, Lincoln was heavily guarded all around, and they knew it was inviolable. Therefore, they had to make a second plan. After a few days, some of Mr. de Valera's party members dressed up as farmers and went to cultivate near Lincoln Prison. When they had time, they sang rural songs next to the prison. Sometimes they mixed in Gaelic slang. Irish villagers liked to sing, so the jailers didn't care. They did not know that Mr. de Valera's party had used Gaelic to convey orders and communicate with each other in the singing. Therefore, Mr. de Valera knew everything in prison about how to arrange things outside the prison. Mr. de Valera was ordered by the rescuers to make a seal of the key to the main gate after prison and throw it in the field. So the fake key was also completed. But how to deal with the armed guards? A solution was soon found.

Random Thoughts on Freedom

— Guan Chonglou

The explanation of the word freedom is that life should be based on the individual as a unit, and everything must be decided by oneself, and cannot be restricted by others. If life does not get freedom, it is like a bird in a cage, losing the joy of survival. So the two sentences (It is better to die than to be unfree) are for those who have lost their freedom.

A puppet can be manipulated by others. A zombie can be manipulated by others. Puppets and zombies are things that have lost their freedom. (If you lose your freedom, you might as well die cleanly.) From this point I can not help but think of those puppets and zombies of the three northeastern provinces.

Freedom has its limits. As the Western saying goes (The definition of freedom refers to not infringing on the freedom of others.) It can be seen that if you want freedom, you must first respect the freedom of others. Japan's dispatch of troops to our country this time is justified in order to protect overseas Chinese and to stop the boycott of Japanese goods. The purpose is nothing more than to allow Japanese people to act freely in China and Japanese goods to be sold freely in China. However, the result of Japan's dispatch of troops this time was the massacre of many of our people and the destruction of much of our property. And the anti-Japanese movement became more and more intense in our country. This is a lesson. (Seeking freedom by force is counterproductive.) So the Japanese want to achieve their freedom through aggression, but it will only see them exhausted.

All living beings in the world with souls are yearning for freedom. All oppressed nations in the world are yearning to break away from the shackles of imperialists. (Ideals are the mother of facts.) A life of freedom and equality will always be realized in the near future that we expect.

Chinese Daughters

— Lu Pin

"Shina" (支那) is a contemptuous and frivolous name for us by the Japanese. But I am now using it to title my article to use it as an encouragement. Liu Dajie wrote patriotic novels and used it as the title of his book, which is also based on this purpose. Last year, during the Northeast Incident, although our authorities adhered to a non-resistance policy, public sentiment was boiling, and young people rose up to join the army. The talents of women were no less than those of men. When the Shanghai Aid-Ma Troupe set out, there were female group members participating. Women in military gear became a beautiful story. It is a pity that the group did not cross the border and eventually dispersed. After the Shanghai Incident, there were female warriors in Feng Dayi's volunteer army and the Tianjin Skull Troupe who defended and killed the enemy, no different from men. And there are many unnamed heroines who work for the country directly or indirectly, anytime and anywhere. A few days ago, I read a Japanese newspaper with a Shanghai communication saying that they had found the diary of a Chinese female soldier, and were surprised and convinced by it. From now on, the Eastern Ocean dwarfs (Japanese) will no longer dare to underestimate Chinese daughters.

Tea, Wine, and Parasitic Diseases

— Bicheng

▲Tea Worm During the Qianlong era of the Qing Dynasty, Mao Shenfu of Wujiang was very fond of tea. He would drink several bowls at a time. Whenever he went out, he would wrap a small amount of tea in paper and place it in his sleeve, taking it out to chew and swallow from time to time. Throughout the year, his face was sallow and emaciated, as if he were ill. Later, this suddenly stopped. When asked, he said, "One year, while on a boat, I leaned against the railing and vomited. Suddenly, a worm emerged from my throat, its color jade green, several inches long, and floated away with the current. Since then, I have no longer been fond of tea, and my complexion has gradually become rosy. Later, he lived to be over eighty years old, and his spirit was still vigorous. It is thought that the worm he vomited was probably of the same type as the 'second peck' mentioned in the Qing Yi Lu."

▲Wine Turtle Some years ago, during a banquet at the Zhang residence in Wumen, a guest spoke of the Wine Turtle, which was very strange. The guest was from Guangfu, and said that there was a carpenter in his village named Jia, who was very fond of wine. All his wages were paid to the wine shop. Over time, he became ill and was unable to work. His family of several nearly froze and starved. After a long illness without a cure, one day, Jia happened to be at his doorstep when a wandering monk passed by. The monk looked closely at Jia and said, "Are you sick from wine?" Jia said, "Yes." The monk said, "I can cure it, but it will be slightly painful, but only for a moment. Can you endure it?" Jia's wife was also beside him, and both said they could endure it. They asked how much the reward would be. The monk said he didn't care about it. So the couple were happy. They asked how to cure it. The monk said, "It must be in an empty room, and I will do as I see fit." They agreed. He ordered them to tie Jia's hands and feet with rope. His wife hesitated. Jia said, "I will die from the illness anyway. I am not afraid." After being tied up, he was ordered to lie on the ground, and a bowl of good wine was placed in front of him. Jia smelled the wine, and saliva dripped from his mouth. After a while, his stomach began to hurt. After a long time, the pain became more severe, reaching his chest. He cried out for help. The monk warned him not to move, saying, "Do not let the effort be wasted. Endure it a little longer, and it will be over." After another while, a turtle, the size of a silver coin, emerged from his mouth and jumped into the bowl of wine, its back black and its belly purple, swimming in the wine. The monk immediately untied him, and the pain was as if it had disappeared. After that, his illness gradually healed, and he no longer liked wine.

The Future of Film

— Lü Bing

I once read an American magazine in which the great inventor Thomas Edison said in a speech that the invention and progress of film, according to his ideal, could be divided into three stages. From moving performances to transmitting sound, it could be said that the second stage had already been successfully achieved. In the future, further research and improvements could eliminate the need for a screen and allow for screenings anywhere. With a simple adjustment, the film would appear, and viewers would feel as if they could touch the events on the screen. Only then would it reach the realm of marvel. At the time, some listeners thought it could not be achieved, and after Edison's death, many doubted that this ideal could be realized. Unexpectedly, news recently came from England that the art of aerial imaging had been largely completed by scientists in that country. When it is made public to the world in the future, the word "screen" will no longer be applicable. This is a novel matter, and I know that those who are addicted to movies will surely want to see it first. According to the original text, after the invention of film, deficiencies were noticed. One of these was that the screen projection was always on a flat surface and could not be viewed from the side at will. This differed from looking at ordinary pictures through a magnifying glass only in whether it was moving or not. Therefore, can the films shown on the market today be called realistic? In the near future, we will see the emergence of the latest type of film, which is easy to use and, when shown, can make the audience think that the actors are performing live, and not from a film. It has already undergone many tests and can truly be called lifelike. Currently, the inventor mentioned above has not disclosed the secret of aerial imaging. The detailed content cannot be explored. What is known is that this type of film does not use a screen. Any part of the hall or reception room can be used for projection. The scenery and actors are all in the air. The projector is equipped with various optical lenses, presumably using the principle of light wave refraction.

Record of the Rongma Shuanglou (51)

— Master of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Seven: Seeking Favor Reaches the Door, Often Causing the General to Stumble; Imprisonment in Love's Jail, the Jailer Can Be a Husband's Cage. It is said that in Beijing City, there is a most famous Jinxiangyu Hutong. There are many large mansions connected in the hutong, but the largest and most extravagant one is the newly built Ye Residence. It was the new residence built by Military Governor Ye Zuozhang. He spent countless sums of money to build this residence into a luxurious and extravagant place. It can even be regarded as a combination of Chinese and Western styles and a complete collection of architecture. Chinese styles such as the large courtyard, opera stage, garden, pavilions, and terraces are all available. There are also two Western-style buildings with complete facilities such as restaurants, dance halls, bathrooms, and ballrooms. Almost all kinds of Chinese and Western buildings can be found as a specimen in his residence. Although it encompasses everything and can be called grand, it is a pity that it is too discordant, like a bowl of potpourri. Since its completion, he himself has been a military governor in other provinces and rarely comes to Beijing. In total, he has not lived in this house for more than ten days. This time, he came to Beijing to participate in some military and political conferences, and he arrived with great fanfare, staying in this house. Unconsciously, half a month passed. This time, the hutong became even more lively. Every day, from morning to night, the traffic was very crowded, almost bursting the narrow hutong. These were all kinds of people entering and leaving the Ye Residence, vying to serve and cater to him, creating a scene of prosperity. Sometimes, if there was a big banquet or a major celebration in the Ye Residence, there were too many guests, and it was necessary to specify a traffic route. A team of armed military police guarded the east entrance of the hutong, near the main road, and only allowed cars to enter. Other carriages and rickshaws required guests to get out and walk. Furthermore, they were only allowed to enter, not exit. Cars leaving the Ye Residence had to detour out of the west entrance and take another route. There were also sentry posts and military police at the west entrance to supervise and direct traffic. Often, they were still taking care of things late into the night, and the cars were still honking incessantly, disturbing the nearby neighbors who couldn't get a good night's sleep. One day, around four o'clock in the afternoon, cars were arriving one after another outside the gate of the Ye Residence, carrying who knows how many strange guests. However, there was only one car from which a graceful and beautiful female guest stepped out. Two idle soldiers standing outside the gate glanced at her and whispered to each other, "The superiors haven't called for any passes yet. This woman seems to be new. But she's really pretty and has quite an air about her. Doesn't look like someone from a brothel, but she doesn't have any attendants either. What kind of person is she?" As they spoke, the female guest walked slowly and entered the gate.

Science

The Method of Making Soap

— Yue Zhao

In the year 79 of the Western calendar, the writings of the Westerner Pliny the Elder recorded that the Colombians invented a method of mixing wood ash and lime in water to form a solution of potassium hydroxide (Potassium Hydroxide, the molecular formula is KOH). When this solution is cooked with oils and fats to a suitable temperature, the fire is removed, allowing it to cool and solidify, thus becoming washing soap.

The factories of various countries now follow this method. However, sodium hydroxide (Sodium Chloride molecule, or NaOH) is used instead of potassium hydroxide because the properties of sodium hydroxide and potassium hydroxide are exactly the same. During manufacturing, butter (pork fat can also be used) is placed in a pot and heated to gradually melt it. After it has completely melted, the sodium hydroxide solution is poured into the pot, stirring vigorously to mix it with the butter. After foam appears on the surface of the liquid, the fire is extinguished, these foams are removed, and pure salt is added to the pot, stirring in the same way. After some time, white powder floats up. Then, these powders are placed in a mold, and when they are cold, they gradually solidify, becoming ordinary laundry soap.

The method of making scented soap is the same as that of ordinary soap. However, after adding salt, the floating white powder must be taken out, washed with clean water, and then heated to boiling, injecting fragrances or disinfectant medicines, and then placed in a mold. When it cools and solidifies, it becomes scented soap.

Why can soap wash away dirt? This is because soap is made of butter and sodium hydroxide. When it encounters water, part of it decomposes into sodium hydroxide, and part of it decomposes into fatty acids. The sodium hydroxide contains saltiness and can combine with dirt, sinking to the bottom of the water; it can also create large bubbles, sticking and floating dirt on the surface of the water: fatty acids are very greasy and can help with washing. Therefore, soap is a necessity for washing.

In addition to washing with soap, soda ash and lye can also be used for washing. Because soda ash and lye both contain alkalinity, their dirt-removing effects are similar to those of soap, but without the help of fatty acids. Moreover, they contain too much alkalinity, which can easily damage the washed objects, so this cannot be ignored.

Bamboo Shaped Wood Shavings

The Cab Driver Class and the "Pig" Slogan

— Ying Dai

As a streetcar sped forward, a car suddenly cut in front of it at an intersection. The streetcar driver quickly slammed on the brakes, avoiding a collision. The streetcar driver, because the car driver had delayed his time and route, would naturally curse, "Pig!" At that time, the car driver, to avoid a fine, could only silently accept the elegant title of "Pig."

As a car was speeding forward, a rickshaw puller suddenly pulled a rickshaw, blocking his way. After the car driver braked, he would naturally curse, "Pig!" The rickshaw puller was smart, knowing that the car carried rich and powerful people, so how dare he argue with the car driver? Under the title of "Pig," he could only silently run away.

As a rickshaw was passing, the puller was using all his strength to desperately pull the rickshaw forward, suddenly a small cart driver came from the opposite direction, his cart was full of seven or eight bags of rice, and he was slowly pushing the cart like an ant, with sweat pouring down his forehead. Luckily, the rickshaw puller was quick and stopped, otherwise he would collide with the small cart. At that time, the rickshaw puller, in great anger, would also naturally curse at the small cart driver, "Pig!" The small cart driver and the rickshaw puller were originally unfortunate coolies, but comparatively, the rickshaw puller was slightly higher up, so the small cart driver only accelerated his pace and pushed forward, not arguing with the rickshaw puller and silently accepting the title of "Pig."

We only need to live in Shanghai for a few years to often see this situation on the road. Here, we can also see that the class among the car drivers is also very clear. In addition, when pedestrians cross the road and are almost crushed under the wheels of a speeding streetcar or car, after escaping with their lives, the streetcar or car driver will curse, "Pig!" Under the shock, the person is still trembling, his mind is not settled, so naturally he does not care that someone is giving him the title of "Pig." There are many vulgar phrases for cursing people, but the first sentence that car drivers curse is usually "Pig," so the two words "Pig" have invisibly become the common slogan for car drivers to curse people. This is also a fine structure in Shanghai's unique art of cursing, right?

A Corner of Society

Faithful Believer

— Lao Tang

A few strands of tempting gongs and drums drifted in the wind, attracting another me, a "sightseeing" Buddha, to the Jing'an Temple on the Bathing Buddha Festival.

After seeing the big wooden fish in the corridor, I ran into the house with the words "Great Hero Hall" hanging at the entrance.

The house was filled with seventeen or eighteen girls shaking their big butts, old women with bound feet reciting Amitabha Buddha, various bosses who came specifically to find the God of Wealth (at the incense and candle place), and workers who reeked of alcohol and garlic and were too unpleasant to approach.

The atmosphere was extremely tense, the smoke was extremely diffuse. Here, the sincere seeking minds of ordinary incense burners and the critical gazes of onlookers are all offered before the "Greatly Compassionate Avalokiteśvara Bodhisattva." The Bodhisattva still lowers her eyebrows and is merciful, her big belly is inclusive, and her smile is amiable, as if saying (you general foolish men and women).

Suddenly, "Amitabha Buddha" filled the entire Great Hero Hall. Looking back, a young man in a suit and a modern girl were bowing deeply before the majestic Bodhisattva, without any regard for the tightly permed hair on their heads and the straight line of their suit pants.

Driven by curiosity, I approached him and her (apparently a couple) who were silently chanting something in their mouths.

The monk ran eagerly in front of them, seemingly waiting for a very great hope to arrive.

Several colorful banknotes, from the hand of the young man in the suit, to the hand of the monk with the bald head, then the sound of (benevolent and generous) (Bodhisattva bless you) replaced the sound of (Amitabha Buddha) just now, and filled the entire house.

The monk, full of spring breeze, took the banknotes and asked the young man's (honorable last name) (first name). He - that young man took out a business card unhurriedly and handed it to the monk's outstretched hand.

Although the eyes, blinded by the smoke, were not far from that business card, but because the time was short, I only saw two words. I didn't remember these two words wrong: (Ling Jing).

Walking out of the temple door, it seemed that I could still hear the young man asking: (Is there an Old Man Under the Moon here)?

On the way home, I recited in my mouth (faithful believer) (Bodhisattva's) (faithful believer)! (Modern girl's)!

Respectfully inform you that my little son ×× and little daughter ×× are now engaged with pain on the day of the National Humiliation Day of May 9th through the introduction of Mr. ×× and Mr. ××. Certainly There

In the Streetcar

— Jie

Most people who have lived in Shanghai for a long time know how difficult it is to travel in Shanghai, and it is especially dangerous in buses and streetcars. If your pocket bulges, no matter what is inside, you must be patronized by friends who specialize in opening boxes, and if you wear a beautiful hat and sit in the streetcar, it will disappear in an instant when the car passes through an intersection, leaving you watching it fly away and crying in vain.

Last Friday night, I took the streetcar from Cadre Road to Stealing Chicken Bridge because of something. After a few stops, the passengers gradually became crowded. Soon, two friends in black gowns walked in from the third-class car and stood in front of me. They did not buy tickets. I thought they must have monthly tickets, right? When the car arrived at Nicheng Bridge, one of them jumped off. In an instant, the car arrived at Stealing Chicken Bridge, and the passengers went down one after another. Finally, I also stood up to prepare to go down. Unexpectedly, the friend in front of me deliberately stood in front of me. I suddenly felt a hand touching my pocket. Looking back, the fountain pen inserted in my pocket was missing! I suddenly realized the reason why those two friends wanted to be my temporary bodyguards.

So, I turned around quickly and grabbed the suspected pickpocket next to me. He was also very calm and lifted his robe, letting me search. However, those with experience told me that searching is useless. There is not just one pickpocket. Who can be sure that he didn't pass the stolen goods to someone else?

(I have been telling you passengers to be careful of your pockets...) As I got off the car, the ticket seller said loudly, showing his duty to serve. In fact, he never cared about me like that, and while I asked him to open the door slowly so that I had a chance to catch and search, he still opened the door, letting the pickpocket escape!

In the end, is it that the friends who freeload in society are afraid of their power? Or is it like the (officials protecting each other) on the political stage? I doubted.

▲Criminal Instructions▲

Regarding Xu Yang Shi petitioning that her son Xu Ruyou was accused of theft.

Request to permit bail and declare innocence. Upon reviewing the petition, your son Xu Ruyou confessed to the crime of theft in court and was sentenced on the 9th of this month. The request shall not be considered. This instruction issued.

Regarding Yang Daosheng petitioning to sue Ni Wenqing for fraud. Please issue a summons and a certificate for arrest so that the accused may be arrested at any time. Upon reviewing the petition, although it is said that the defendant is often seen in Shanghai, since there is no definite time or place, the whereabouts are still unclear. The request to issue a summons and a certificate for arrest so that the accused may be arrested at any time cannot be approved. Received and filed.

▲ Wang Linqi vs. Wang Xinggao, etc. Inheritance Case (Main Text) The seventy-one mu, four fen, one li, and five hao of Qingyi farmland, twenty-five mu, one fen, one li, and four hao of Shangyi farmland, nine residential rooms, and twelve market rooms left by Wang Qinxiang shall be inherited by the plaintiff. The defendant, Wang Xiaochuan, shall return twenty shi of rent rice received from Wu Dahe to the plaintiff. The rest of the plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The plaintiff shall return the nine residential rooms to the defendant, Wang Rongfu. The rest of the counterclaim by the defendant Wang Rongfu and the counterclaim by the defendant Wang Xiaozhi are both dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants Wang Xinggao, Wang Rongfu, and Wang Xiaozhi in the proportions of 3/10 each, and by the plaintiff in the proportion of 1/10. The counterclaim costs shall be borne by the defendant Wang Xiaozhi in the proportion of 8/10, and by the defendant Wang Rongfu and the plaintiff in the proportion of 1/10 each.

▲ Criminal Judgment: Yang Shusheng et al. Opium Case (Main Text) Yang Shusheng, intending to profit, opened a shop for people to smoke opium, sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Also, for smoking opium, sentenced to three months of imprisonment. The combined sentence is eight months of imprisonment. The number of days in detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Mao Mingqing and Lu Wenkui, for smoking opium, are sentenced to two months of imprisonment, with a two-year suspended sentence. The number of days in detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated.

▲ Tang Jilin Theft (Main Text) Tang Jilin committed theft during a disaster and is sentenced to six months of imprisonment. The number of days in detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲ Gao Yisheng Assault Case (Main Text) Gao Yisheng assaulted another person's body and is sentenced to forty days of detention. The number of days in detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲ Criminal Instruction: Yu Zhoushi accuses Yang Sanhe et al. of kidnapping her daughter and assault. It has been noted that the accuser accused Yang Sanhe et al. of kidnapping her daughter and then requested to withdraw the accusation, showing that the accusation is not entirely true. The accusation of kidnapping and the accusation of assault should be dismissed. Let it be known. This instruction.

▲ Gu Liusheng continues to request an investigation. It has been noted that the current residence or location of the defendants in this case is located at Avenue Edward VII, which is under the jurisdiction of the Special District Court. The request to propose an investigation cannot be approved. Continue to follow the previous instruction. This instruction.

▲ Yu Changshengqing requests a temporary halt to detention. It has been noted that the civilian in this case has already withdrawn the appeal and the ruling has already been submitted. The request to come to the court for bail and temporarily restore freedom should be postponed. This instruction. (May 13)
